    WHERE [c].[IsDeleted] IS NULL AND ([c].[ContentTypesId] = @__selectid_0)
    ORDER BY (SELECT 1)
    OFFSET @__p_1 ROWS
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [l].[Id], [l].[Code], [l].[CreaDate], [l].[CreaUser], [l].[IsDefault], [l].[IsDeleted], [l].[IsStatus], [l].[LoginCount], [l].[ModDate], [l].[ModUser], [l].[Name], [l].[OrderNo]

) AS [t0] ON [t].[LangId] = [t0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c0].[Id], [c0].[BannerButtonText], [c0].[BannerText], [c0].[ButtonLink], [c0].[ButtonText], [c0].[ContentData], [c0].[ContentOrderNo], [c0].[ContentPageId], [c0].[ContentShort], [c0].[ContentTypesId], [c0].[CreaDate], [c0].[CreaUser], [c0].[Description], [c0].[EndDate], [c0].[ExternalLink], [c0].[FormTypeId], [c0].[IsActive], [c0].[IsClick], [c0].[IsDeleted], [c0].[IsFooterMenu], [c0].[IsGallery], [c0].[IsHamburgerMenu], [c0].[IsHeaderMenu], [c0].[IsHome], [c0].[IsMap], [c0].[IsPublish], [c0].[IsSideMenu], [c0].[IsStatus], [c0].[LangId], [c0].[Link], [c0].[LoginCount], [c0].[MetaDescription], [c0].[MetaKeywords], [c0].[MetaTitle], [c0].[ModDate], [c0].[ModUser], [c0].[Name], [c0].[OrderNo], [c0].[OrjId], [c0].[OrjId1], [c0].[StartDate], [c0].[TemplateType], [c0].[VideoLink]
    FROM [ContentPage] AS [c0]
    WHERE [c0].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t1] ON [t].[ContentPageId] = [t1].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [c1].[Id], [c1].[CreaDate], [c1].[CreaUser], [c1].[Description], [c1].[IsDeleted], [c1].[IsStatus], [c1].[LoginCount], [c1].[ModDate], [c1].[ModUser], [c1].[Name], [c1].[OrderNo]
    FROM [ContentTypes] AS [c1]
    WHERE [c1].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t2] ON [t].[ContentTypesId] = [t2].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d].[Id], [d].[Alt], [d].[BannerImageId], [d].[CreaDate], [d].[CreaUser], [d].[DocumentId], [d].[GalleryId], [d].[Guid], [d].[IsDeleted], [d].[IsStatus], [d].[Link], [d].[LoginCount], [d].[ModDate], [d].[ModUser], [d].[Name], [d].[OrderNo], [d].[PictureId], [d].[ThumbImageId], [d].[Title], [d].[Types], [d].[data_class]
    FROM [Documents] AS [d]
    WHERE [d].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t3] ON [t].[Id] = [t3].[DocumentId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c2].[Id], [c2].[BannerButtonText], [c2].[BannerText], [c2].[ButtonLink], [c2].[ButtonText], [c2].[ContentData], [c2].[ContentOrderNo], [c2].[ContentPageId], [c2].[ContentShort], [c2].[ContentTypesId], [c2].[CreaDate], [c2].[CreaUser], [c2].[Description], [c2].[EndDate], [c2].[ExternalLink], [c2].[FormTypeId], [c2].[IsActive], [c2].[IsClick], [c2].[IsDeleted], [c2].[IsFooterMenu], [c2].[IsGallery], [c2].[IsHamburgerMenu], [c2].[IsHeaderMenu], [c2].[IsHome], [c2].[IsMap], [c2].[IsPublish], [c2].[IsSideMenu], [c2].[IsStatus], [c2].[LangId], [c2].[Link], [c2].[LoginCount], [c2].[MetaDescription], [c2].[MetaKeywords], [c2].[MetaTitle], [c2].[ModDate], [c2].[ModUser], [c2].[Name], [c2].[OrderNo], [c2].[OrjId], [c2].[OrjId1], [c2].[StartDate], [c2].[TemplateType], [c2].[VideoLink]
    FROM [ContentPage] AS [c2]
    WHERE [c2].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t4] ON [t].[Id] = [t4].[ContentPageId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t0].[Id], [t1].[Id], [t2].[Id], [t3].[Id], [t4].[Id]"
